28a4(phal chen): sa rnams kun dang rjes su ldan// bdag med nyid rtog/ sa 'od kyang btang snyoms byed pa min// de dag snying brtse gcig tu gsal bar chos kyang brjod/ 
28a5(phal chen): 'on kyang dmigs par mi gnas de dag 'jig rten rgyu/ de dag 'od zer dra ba sna tshogs mdog bkye zhing / 'gro ba'i mun pa bsal te kun tu snang byas nas// 'od zer
28a6(phal chen): sgo'i pad+mo dag la rgyal sras rnams// kun tu bstan de rdul dang bral ba'i chos kyang ston/ spu gcig rtsel zhing rnams rgyal bas brgyan pa dang // de bzhin rgyal
28a7(phal chen): pa'i sras kyi brgyan par mngon par mthong // 'khor rnams blo sems gzhan dang gzhan can dpe med pa/ 'gro ba de dag sems shes rmongs med ston pa byed/ 
28a8(phal chen): sems 'jug gcig gis phyogs rnams bcu po thams cad kyi// brjod du med pa khrag khrig zhing rnams kun bgrod cing // song ste sangs rgyas 'gro ba'i don du mchod byas nas/ 
28b1(phal chen): drig zag khrig do dang ldan pa sna tshogs 'd-i/ bdag shegs rnams la ba'i 'du shes ter gzhag cing / chos kyi gter ma pas cag tu shes rab rnon po can// ye shes 'byung
28b2(phal chen): gdas pakhas bas sangs rgyas chags med byed/ 'gro ba din 'dong byang chub ba tshig gi snang ba sgrub// gang rnams chas dbyings rnam par bya zhing bas ma byas kyang / 'an la pa
28b3(phal chen): mang po 'das byas rang bar mgyur te// chos nyid gnas med gang lo 'du chung bar mamyor kyangachags med 'i shes can rnam mo skye sems ming par spyod // dus gsul
28b4(phal chen): rgyal ba'i rigs su rigs dang ldan gyur cing / bde gshegs kun gyi sku las yang dag byung gyur bas // chos kyi lus can de dag 'gro la gzugs lus sgom/ 
28b5(phal chen): sgra mkhar mkhas pa yid 'ong sgyu me ston pa bzhin/ mkhas pa de dag la lang spyod pa mchog snying sdang / la yang mkhas pa skye zhing mya ngan 'das par snang / 
28b6(phal chen): byang chub dam pa'i mchog kyang rnam par 'arang rgya sdang / mya ngan 'da' ba ston pa'ang de bzhin lo lar snang / rang rgyal rnams dang nyan thos rgyal po'i sa med pa'i// chos nyid de la/ 
28b7(phal chen): ji ltar rab tu gnas pa ltos// lus dang sgra med bsam med 'du shes ldan pa min// 'on kyang bya ba sna tshogs du ma nye bar ston// 'gro bar chos rnams rnam par 'byed cing
28b8(phal chen): skyer gyur to// 'jig rten gtso bo mi gzugs phyin rgyal sras rnams chags med mthar phyin pa'i ye shes gnas bcas te/ sangs rgyas byin brlabs rnam par 'phrul ba dag
29a1(phal chen): kyang ston/ 'jig rten 'di na de dag 'dra ba gang yang med// de dag pas kyang 'phags pa lta sa zhig spros// thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes yangs pa ma thob par/ 
29a2(phal chen): thams cad mkhyen pa'i thabs su rnam 'phrul mchog kyang thob// gang rnams chos rab 'phags par rtag tu 'jug byed pa// de dag chos rab dam pa mchog gi theg pa yin// 'jig rten
29a3(phal chen): dus dang dus min chod kyang shes byas shing // de dag 'gro la phan phyir rnam par 'phrul pa ston// dpa' bo gang rnams zhing kun bdag gi lus 'gengs shing // gang rnams 'jig
29a4(phal chen): rten 'od zer dra ba mchog gtong ba// mun pa bsal cing snang bas 'jig rten rgyas par byed/ klu'i dbang po bzhin du chos kyi char pa 'bebs// rmi lam
29a5(phal chen): lta bu log pa'i sgyu ma 'dra ba yi// 'du byed rab tu shes nas las rnams sbyor 'jug cing // 'gro ba tham sa cang snying rje chen pos khyab byas nas// rang bzhin
29a6(phal chen): dag pa thar lam bya ba med pa ston// gang rnams rgyal ba'i stobs rnams ji bzhin tshad med dang // gang rnams mkha' ltar 'gro ba kun tu mtha' yas shing // gang rnams sems
29a7(phal chen): can khams kun yongs su dgrol brtson pa// de dag bskal pa bye ba grangs med spyad pa spyod// las mchog bla na med pa shin tu sbyang ba yis// yon tan dam pa sna tshogs rnams kyang/ 
29a8(phal chen): kun sems shing // byang chub sems dpa' de dag spyod pa mchog mi mthong // thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye she 'byung ba rnam par lta// sems 'byung gcig gis 'jig rten bsam gyis mi/ 
29b1(phal chen): khyab pa// 'bum klas kun tu rgyu zhing 'gro ba rab tu snang // tog dang rnam rtog mi byed dag pa'i sems dang ldan// de dag gcig mini lus la lus gcig ston pa byed// de dag 'jig rten
29b2(phal chen): kun la rtog par mi byed de// mgon po kun gyi chos nyid yongs su mi rtog go// de dag chos kun rnams 'byed 'dod chags bral gyur kyang // 'gro ba thar par bya ba yongs su mi
29b3(phal chen): gtong ngo // 'jig rten kun gyi 'du shes rnam pa gang yod pa// bzang ngan 'bring dang de bzhin chung dang sna tshogs kyis// 'du shes thibs po dag dang rab rgol rnam phye ste/ 
29b4(phal chen): de dag byin brlabs rnam par 'phrul pa shin tu ston// ji lta sgyu ma rnam pa sna tshogs tshad med pa// de 'dra'i rnam par 'phrul pas chos dbyings 'di dag 'gengs/ 
29b5(phal chen): namakha'i dbyings kyi mthas klas lus kyi bye brag gis/ 'gro ba rnams kyi mos pa ji bzhin bston pa byed/ de dag gang la'ang ma chags rtogs dang rnam rtogs med/ 
29b6(phal chen): dog pa med cing nyon mongs de bzhir rlom sems med// de dag sangs rgyas chags pa'i blo med thar la min// 'gro ba kun la'ang bde ba'i 'du shes rab tu skyed// 'jig rten kun
29b7(phal chen): nashes la mkhas rab mi 'jigs pa// 'jig rten 'du shes gnas la 'jug par mi byed de// de dag chos kun 'di la 'du shes gang zhes rtog/ de ltar gzhigs na dus gsum
29b8(phal chen): gang yang dmigs pa med// sngon gyi mthar thug 'das pa'i dus la rab zhugs te// phyi ma'i mthar thug ma 'ongs pa la rab zhugs nas// zhing rnams kun na ci yod kun
30a1(phal chen): kyang de bzhin du// shin tu shes kyang rtag par gang yang mi dmigs so// mya ngan 'das pa'i dbyings la'ang brtson par de bzhin gnas// nyon mongs med pa'i
30a2(phal chen): tshul gyi rjes song mi gnas te// de dag yang dag mtha' 'dra la 'dra ba med// byang chub spyod pa las kyang dpa' bo mi ldog go// gang rnams byang chub brtan pa'i ri rab bzhin gnas
30a3(phal chen): shing / sangs rgyas rgyal sras mkhas pas chos dbyings thams cad dang // 'gro ba kun tu shin tu gang byas pa// 'di ni dpa' bo rnams kyi spyod pa'i mchog yin no// blo mchog das
30a4(phal chen): pag zhig thams cad mkhyen pa yi// rnam grol mdzes dpa'i tshul mchog yang ba 'dod pa ni// des ni gang las zag zang srod gsum pade 'byung ba'i/ byang chu
30a5(phal chen): sems la rim pa med par 'jug par gyis// gang gi bsam pa rdul bral byang chub sems gnas pa/ de dag yon tan legs pa zad par brjod mi nus// 'on
30a6(phal chen): kyang 'gro ba'i don du bde gshegs legs brjod phyir// yon tan ldan pa de'i spyod pa mchog kyang nyon// gang gis zhing rnams bye ba khrag khrig rdul byas te// phyogs rnams re re kun
30a7(phal chen): du bkang ste dgrang byas shing // de'i rjes su dpag pas rnam 'dren zad byed na// 'du shes rnams ni mthar thugs zad par mi 'gyur ro// gang zhig sems can grangs ma khas
30a8(phal chen): sems can 'du shes med spyod pa tsam du gzhol zhing sgra la ma chags par// gang zhig 'jig rten ma khams 'byed chags pa med pa'i sems// de dag ldang dang grangs mkhas grangs dmigs/ 
30b1(phal chen): meng pa yid// sad kyi rnam pa'i dbyangs ni mthara' las rgya che dang // dus rnams 'jig rten kun tu rtogs pa'i mkhas pa gang // slar mos thal gtor bzhin du 'i com rnam gtor ba
30b2(phal chen): de dag sangs rgyas chos rtogs yid can chags pa med// gang dag phyogs rnams mtha' yas zhing la rab 'jug cing // sems bskyed gcig gis blo nyams med par 'dod byed pa/ 
30b3(phal chen): de dag tha dad grangs ltogs pas der zhugs te// skye ba med pa'i chos la yang dag mtha' ltar mkhas// gang zhig sangs rgyas bye ba khrag khrig pasam yas pa'i// 'khor du nye bar
30b4(phal chen): phyin te zham ring 'khor gnas shing // gtso bo dag la 'dri ba'i thog mar gang 'gro ba// spyod yul mchog can de'i smon lam mchog 'di yin// gang zhig
30b5(phal chen): phyogs rnams kun gyi mgon po kun dran zhing // chos nyid de la nam yang gnas par ma gyur pa// khams gsum dge ba gang yod kun gyi rgyu yin te// de dag zhing
30b6(phal chen): rnams thams cad yongs su dag par sbyong // gang rnams skye ba'i rgyud du srid gsum sna tshogs rnams// 'jig rten kun na yod la ma chags mig gyur pa// de dag bag chags
30b7(phal chen): mkhas shing de bzhin dbang po mkhas// mos pa bye ba khrag khrog bsam yas de bzhin mkhas// 'gro ba'i bsam pa ji bzhin gang gis shes gyur cing // shes rab chen po de dag
30b8(phal chen): de bzhin chos ston pa// de dag kun nas nyon mongs rnams dag tshul la mkhas// sems can mang po rnam par sbyong ba'i lam ldan ston// gang zhig ting 'dzin bye ba khrag khrig
31a1(phal chen): tsung byas rnams sems rgyub gcig gis rjes sa rnags gyur pa/ dedag sa nam sna tshags gnas par rab tu shes// ldang ba'i rnal
31a2(phal chen): mkhas shing blo gros spyod yul shes// chags med byang chub de la mngon du gang zhugs shing // 'grol phan pa'i don du dri yangs su zhugs pa// ye shes 'byam klas 'di dang
31a3(phal chen): de dag ldan pa yin// de phyir de dag skyes bu mchog gi gsung yang sgrog/ gang zhig bskal pa ring dang bskal pa thung mkhas shing // nyin zhag mkhas shing de bzhin zla ba zla byed mkhas// 
31a4(phal chen): gang yang 'jig rten rtag tu skye ba mkhas byung ba// ning gi rnam pa mkhas shing rnam bya'i chos med pa'o// gang rnams phyogs la zhugs te phyogs kyi rjes 'brang zhing / 
31a5(phal chen): phyogs kun tshad ni rjes su shes par mgyur pa// de dag dbu mas phyogs kyi rjes su 'gro byed cing / zhing rnams sbyong yang yongs su dag rtogs chags pa med/ 
31a6(phal chen): stobs la 'jug pas rgyal ba rnams kyi stobs shes pas// 'gro ba rnams kyi gnas dang gnas min bsam byas na/ 'das dang sa 'os dkar byung ba'i las kyis// yang dag
31a7(phal chen): rtogs byas las kyi rnam par smin la gnas/ 'jig rten kun mkhas sna tshogs tha dang ji bzhin du// sring gsum rnam par rgyu ba'i tshul yang ji bzhin dang // dbang ba rnam/ 
31a8(phal chen): po 'bring dang dbang po tha mar yang // 'gro ba ma lus kun gyi dbang po rnam par 'byed// mos pa rnam pa sna tshogs dge dang mi dge dang // bzang ngan de bzhin 'bring la rnam par/ 
31b1(phal chen): sems byed cing / 'gro ba'i kun du 'gro ba na pa rnam pal byed// slong gsum d+hA'i rgyud kyang de dag rab tu shes/ bsam gtan rnam thar nyon mongs ji bzhin mtshan ma mthong/ 
31b2(phal chen): nyon mongs mtshams sbyor rnam byang cis 'gyur dang // sngan chad gnas kyi bde dang sdug bsngal rgyud rnams kyang // brtan pa rnams ni sangs rgyas stobs rnams sbyong ba byed/ 
31b3(phal chen): ji ltar 'gro ba'i las rgyud nyon mongs las 'jug dang / 'gro rgyud thams cad 'jig cing zhing 'gyur thams cad dang // zag pa sna tshogs rnams kyang ji ltar sbyor 'gyur ba/ 
31b4(phal chen): ngagachags mtshams sbyor rje bzhin de bzhin rab tu 'jug ji ltar 'jig rten nyon mongs zad cing dag 'gyurag/ de la skyes bu khyu mchog spyod pa'i blo dang ldan/ 
31b5(phal chen): stsogs 'chang dag ni stobs bcu rnams kyi 'od sdang ste/ rgyal ba'i rtobs kyang thobs min the tsom yod pa min// spu rtsi gcig la gang rnams rnam par sems
31b6(phal chen): byed cing / tal la nyon mongs la la dag dang yang ba yi/ sna tshogs zhing rnams tshad las 'das po kun mthong nas// las dang bya ba sna tshogs rgyud tu rab
31b7(phal chen): tu shes/ gang rnams rdul gcig rtse la rnams brjod med pa'i// zhing dang bde gshegs sras rnams sems can gtso mthong yang / zhing rnams
31b8(phal chen): 'khrugs shing 'dres pa'i nyes pa gang yang med/ gcig la 'jug pas rnal 'byor ldan pa kun la 'jug/ spu gcig rtse la phyogs bcu thams cad rnams phye ste/ 
32a1(phal chen): na mkha'i dbyings thugs 'jig rten khams rnams kun zhugs shing / phyogs 'ga' tsam yang rgyal bas stong par mthong ba med/ 
32a2(phal chen): de bzhin zhing dang 'jig rten 'byam klas de dag sbyong // bam po nyi shu bzhi pa/ de ltar brtan pas rgyal bas stong min
32a3(phal chen): zhing shes nas// 'jig rten kun kyang spu rtse gcig la yod par 'jug/ dus gsum rgyud rnams mtshan nyid tha dad khams kun dang / nyin zhag dus dang zla phyed rgyud kyi rnam thar
32a4(phal chen): 'jug de ltar rgyal sras 'jigs med byang chub sem das dpa'i rnams/ skyes bu khru mchog ye shes rgyal srid thob zhugs pa/ de dag 'di 'dra shes
32a5(phal chen): nas rjes su sems byed cing / bde gshegs rnams la dga' ba mtha' yas yangs pa 'thob/ gang rnams bye ba khrag khrig sna tshogs lus bsgyur cing / 
32a6(phal chen): phyogs bcu'i rgyal ba thams cad mngon par mchod pa'i phyir/ rnam 'phrul dam pa bzang po kun tu ston byed pa/ de dag mgon po rnams kyi spyod yul rab la zhugs/ 
32a7(phal chen): gang rnams sangs rgyas bye ga khrag khrig drung bslabs shing / gang rnams chos kyi mdzod rtogs yid la ngoms med de/ gang dag mgon po khyu mchog rnams la dga' sems pa/ 
32a8(phal chen): de dag chos kyi sprin yin spyod pa mang la spyod/ ye shes 'phel bar 'gyur ba'i chos kyi gnas mkhas pa/ de dag sangs rgyas 'byung gnas ting 'dzin thob pa yin/ 
32b1(phal chen): ri rgyal lta bu dag dang pa'i 'byung gnas ban/ ye shes 'byung gnas 'gro bar yan tan 'byung gnas so// gnas pa med pa das bzhin tu langs pa dang // thams cad
32b2(phal chen): mkhyen la mngon nur mya ngan med pa dang // sems can stongs cing nyon mongs rtogs pa med zhugs pa'i// byams pa'i bsam pas 'gro ba kun kyang 'gengs// de dag snyi
32b3(phal chen): de'i driya ni kyims payid// bdag ma tshang sangs ngo ban sangs rgyas sems can/ gzhan dunam pa ma bung na nyid me par 'juganyams par gyur
32b4(phal chen): sems can rnams mthong phyir zhing tsam/ dbyang chub sems la mkhas pa dag gi chang dag ni/ bska la pa bye ba'i mthas kyang brjod par mi nus te/ 
32b5(phal chen): ci phyir zhe na de las sangs rgyas thams cad byung / dbang bdes rim gror byas dang rang rgyal kun kyang byung // phyogs bcu'i zhing rnams grangs med bcur ni 'grangs
32b6(phal chen): gyur pa'i// sems can thams cad bskal pa gcig tu bder bkod cing // bslab pa bcu dang dge bcu bsam gtan 'thob pa dang // tshangs pa dag dang rnam grol zhi ba'i gnas
32b7(phal chen): bkod cing // de dag bskal pa byed re rab bkod de// dgra bcom nyon mongs zhi la rab tu dgod byas kyang // byang chub sems dpa' dge ba'i tshogs kyi char mi rung // byang chub
32b8(phal chen): sems dpa' zhugs ma thag tu tshogs chen sog/ nyon mongs med cing shin tu phra lam rtogs pa yi/ rang rgyal sems can bye ba khrag khrig bkod gyur kyang // bsod nams
33a1(phal chen): bsag pa ngas ni byang chub sems rapa la// grangs dang dang bgrang ba'i rnam par nyer mi 'gro/ zhing gi rdul ni chad kyis shes par rung yang snang / nang / 
33a2(phal chen): sems kyis ning mangs yongs su 'das byas shing // de ltar bskal pa brjod las zad par 'gro byas na// ning mtha' thug par rung srid byang chub sems mchog min// mtha'
33a3(phal chen): rnams kun tu bskal pa mang ba'i mnga' med de/ sngon gyi mthar gyur bskal pa de bzhin ma 'ongs dang / nga ltar byung ba'i bskal pa rang dang thug med pa'i/ brgal pa de da
33a4(phal chen): bang sring byang chub sangs ma yid// ci pyir nan 'di sa byugs rnams ca dgang zhing // tog dang rnam rtog yongs su shes par bya ba'i phying / nang cis
33a5(phal chen): gcig gis du gsum rtogs par bya don du/ 'gro/ ba'i don du 'dod cing sems mchog rin chen skye// phyogs bcu'i zhing rnams stong mang kun tu mtha' yas pa'i
33a6(phal chen): 'gro ba rnams kyi mos pa bsam pa ci 'dra dang / sbyor gang dang sems dang spyod pa de bzhin te/ mthar thug rung sring mkha' 'dra'i byang chub sems mtha' min// de ni 'dra/ 
33a7(phal chen): ltar phyogs bcu byams dang snying rje dang / bsam pa chen pos 'gro ba thams cad rgyas byas shing // thar pa'i don du sangs rgyas yon tan kun sbyar phyir// rin chen sems
33a8(phal chen): kyi stobs ni tshad med rab tu skyes/ mas dang bsapa pa yid bzhin yang dag sbyong ba dang // 'gro ba'i dbang bskur ba sems dang spyad pa rnams/ skad cig gcig gis pa
33b1(phal chen): bzhir rtogs par bya ba phyir/ thams cad ma byed pa'i ye shes lta bu'i sems skyes so// 'gro ba'i las dang nyon mongs su tshogs 'byam klas pa// gang gis khams gas
33b2(phal chen): 'di dag tu ni skyer 'gyur ba// de dag mtha' ni phyogs bcur rnyed par rung srid kyi// byang chub sems kyi mchog la kun tu mthar med do// ci phyir zhe na 'di ltar nyon mongs
33b3(phal chen): las bral ba'o// sems ni de bzhin gshegs pa mchod pa'i don du skye/ nyon mongs grol byed de bzhin las kyi rgyud kyang gcod// dus gsum mun pa sel cing mi zang
33b4(phal chen): snying rjes byung / phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas mtha' da yas ma lus thams cad dang / sems can dmang po thams cad sems gcig bskyed pa yis/ 
33b5(phal chen): spos dang me tog phreng ba byug pa dam pa dang // gdug rgyal mtshan bza' btung na bzas mchod par byed/ gzhan yang gdan gyi rnam pa 'chags dam pa dang / 
33b6(phal chen): pho brang mang po sna tshogs can dan mchog bsangs pa// nor bu rin chen rnam par snang bas brgyan pa dang / yid bzhin nor bu yod 'ong brgyan pas mchod byas te// de ltar bde gshegs
33b7(phal chen): sems can mngon par mchod byed pas// bskal pa khrag khrig brjod du med pa zang byas kyang // byang chub sems dpa'i ngade bsams mthar phyin bde ba nyid// gang bsgrubs byang chub sems
33b8(phal chen): la mnyam par nyer mi 'gro// ji snyed dper brjod byas pa'i dag thams cad kyang // yang dag skyes pa'i byang chub sems kyi char mi rung // de yang 'di ltar dus gsum bzhugs
34a1(phal chen): pa'i skyes bu'i mchog thams cang byang chub sems mdzag de las byung ba yin/ byang chub sems ni chags pa med pa'i mamang phyin te// thams cad/ 
34a2(phal chen): tshad la gnas kyang de la tshad yod min// thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes gzhol zhing tshad med stobs// sems can rang bzhin de bzhin byang chub mthar yang phyin// byang chub sems 'di
34a3(phal chen): nam pa'i mtha' dang mnyam pa ste/ chos rnams kun la khyad pa chos dbyings ji bzhin no// tshad med de bzhin nyid kun de'i spyod yul gyur// des ni kun tu khyab pa sems can gtsa/ 
34a4(phal chen): bzhin// de ni 'byam klas chos rnams kun la rjes su nu dgas// des ni zhing rnams ma lus 'byam klas kun de tu khyab// des ni shes pa 'byam klas thams cad rtogs pa
34a5(phal chen): chung// des ni sangs rgyas 'byam klas kun dang 'gal me thob// rtag tu bsod nams bla na med pa dag dang ldan/ de bzhin rtag tu tshul khrims rnam dag mi gnas ldan/ 
34a6(phal chen): rtag tu kun gtong rtag par rab tu dge ba ste// ldog pa med pa'i brtson 'grus mchog dang rab tu ldan// bsam gtan mdzod la rtag par bsam gtan 'jug pa byed// shes rab
34a7(phal chen): shin tu yangs pa dang yang rtag tu ldan// rgyal sras rnams kyis rab dam pa gang yod pa// de dag don du ye shes kun tu bzang po byung // 'gro ba kun na skyes bu'i seng ge gang
34a8(phal chen): bzhugs pa// de dag gis ni byang chub sems rab byin gyis brlabs// ting nge 'dzin dang gzungs kyi dam pas rab tu brgyan// de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam 'phrul rdzu 'phrul rnam pas brgyad// 
34b1(phal chen): 'jig rten kun dang 'gro ba rnams kyi ji tsam tshad// na mkha'i tshad kyang phyog cu dag tu ji tsam pa// de dag pas kyang byang chub sems 'di chad med de// de las skyes bu'i seng ge kun kyang
34b2(phal chen): skyes shing byung // byang chub sems 'di stobs bcu rnams kyi rtsa ba ste// brtan pa bzhi'i gnas yin so sor shes pa'i rtsa// rgyal ba'i chos rnams bcwo brgyad yang dag 'byin pa ste// skyes bu
34b3(phal chen): gtso bos mkhyen par bya ba'i chos kun 'byin// gzugs kyi sku ni mtshan rab rnams kyis bsags pa dang // chos sku mnyam nyid rtog pa mi mnga' brnyes pa dang // 'gro bas mchod pa'i
34b4(phal chen): ye shes chags med gang byung ba// kun gyi rtsa ba 'byungaganas byang chub sems 'di yin// rang rgyal theg pa/ 'byung zhing nyan thos theg pa'ang 'byung // bsam
34b5(phal chen): gtan ting 'dzin bde ba gzugs kyi khams rnams dang / gzugs med khams rnams ting nge 'dzin gyi bde ba dang / kun gyi rtsa ba 'byung gnas byang chub sems mchog 'di yin no// 
34b6(phal chen): mi dang de bzhin lha dbang po'i bde ba dang // lam rgyud sna tshogs kun kyang 'di la shin tu sbyangs// brtson 'grus stobs dang dbang po'i bde ba gang yod pa// kun gyi rtsa ba dang po byang chub
34b7(phal chen): sems 'di yin// ci phyir zhe na 'di ltar byang chub sems bskyed cing // pha rol byin drug brtson par spyad pa rab tu spyod// sems can rnams la'ang spyod pa yang dag rab tu ston// / 
34b8(phal chen): des ni khams gsum 'gro ba'i bde ba kun kyang 'byung // sangs rgyas chags med thugs chung don dam mkhyen pa'i rnams// chos kyi dam pa mchog rnams yang dag kun ston cing // rgya chen nyon
35a1(phal chen): mongs las las sems can dgrol mdzad de// mya ngan 'das pa dam pa mchogs la dgod mdzad pa// ye shes 'od zer 'od yangs nyi ma lta bu ste// 'gro bar
35a2(phal chen): spyod pa dkar pos yongs rgyas zla ba bzhin// yon tan shin tu bsags pa tshang med chu lta bu// dri med chags pa mi mnga' tshang med mkha' dbyings 'dra// gang zhig yon tan mtha'
35a3(phal chen): yas byang chub sems yangs pa// shin tu che zhing bde skyed tshad med smon byed cing // phyi ma'i mthar thug spyod par smon pas su brtson pa// de dag sems can gdul ba'i don phyir rtag tu brtson// / 
35a4(phal chen): 'jig rten 'jam klas thams cad rnam par srung ba'i phyir// smon lam bye ba khrag khrig bsam gyis mi khyab dang / stong pa mtshan ma med pa smon med mi gnas pa'i// smon lam
35a5(phal chen): bye ba brgyas ni sems de dag par 'gyur// chos kyi rang bzhin na mkha' lta bu sus rtogs shing // zhi dang rab zhi nyer zhir thams cad mnyam gzhog pa// de dag chos
35a6(phal chen): grangs khrag khrig bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i// grangs su 'gro la ston kyang de ni gnas pa med// phyogs bcu kun gyi 'jig rten gtso bo ji snyed pa// de dag kun gyis byang chub sems mchog 'di
35a7(phal chen): bsngags ste// yon tan brgya phrag bsam gyis mi khyabs pas kyang brgyan// sems can gtso bzhin yongs dag pha rol phyin pa yin// bskal pa sems can snyed du gal te legs brjod kyang // byang chub
35a8(phal chen): sems rab de la mthar thugs gang yang med// rgyal ba 'byung ba'i rigs chen der ni gang skyes pa// de'i dpe ni khams gsum klongs kyang gang yang med// dus gsum rgyal ba kun gyis gang
35b1(phal chen): zhig rnam bsags pa'i/ byang chub sems rab de la sngon las kun gyi gyis// byang chub sems rab ngam pa de'i bsod nams gter// des ni rgyal sras chags pa med pa rab tu 'thob
35b2(phal chen): 'gro ba'i sems dang spyod pa shes shing mthong rung srid// zhing rnams rdul du blags te bgrangs par nus kyang srid// bar snang sgra yis mnyam par gzhal par nus srid kyi// byang chub
35b3(phal chen): sems mchog yon tan mthar phyin mi nus so// 'di las dus gsum sangs rgyas thams cad rab tu byung // 'di las 'jig rten 'gro ba kun gyi bde ba 'byung // 'di
35b4(phal chen): las rgyal bas bsngags pa'i legs pa thams cad 'byung // 'dis ni sems can gtso bo the tsom med par 'gyur/  / 'dis ni 'jig rten kun gyi bsgrib pa zad par 'gyur/ 
35b5(phal chen): 'dis ni zhing rnams yongs su dag pa'i mchog tu 'gyur/ 'di las 'jig rten dam pa shes dang ldan pa 'byung gang zhig phyogs bcu'i rgyal ba blta bar 'dod pa dang / 
35b6(phal chen): gang zhig byin dang bsod nams mi zad 'jod 'dod dang // gang zhig 'gro ba kun gyi sdu bsngal zlog 'dod pa// des ni yon tan mtha' yas byang chub sems bskung bya// shin tu rgyas pa chen
35b7(phal chen): po'i mdo// / sangs rgyas phal po che zhes bya ba las/ byang chub sems dang sems dang po bskyed pa'i bsod nams kyi phung po'i dpe yang dag par bsags
35b8(phal chen): pab tshigs su bcad pa'i le'u zhes bya ste/ nyi shu gnyis pa'o// / de nas byang chub sems dpa' brtson 'grus blo gros kyis/ byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi blo gros la 'di skad
36a1(phal chen): ces smras so// kye rgyal ba'i sras/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sems bskyed pa rab tu thob pa/ sems dang po bskyed pa la gnas pa/ de ltar
36a2(phal chen): tshad med pa'i bsod nams kyi tshogs dang ldan pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes rgya chen po la yang dag par 'dzegs pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i skyon med pa shin tu chung ba/ 'jig rten kun tu
36a3(phal chen): khring bar byed pa rnam par bzlog pa rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi 'jig rten las 'das pa'i chos nyid kyi rjes su song ba 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar 'byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs
36a4(phal chen): pa thams cad kyis byin gyis brlabs pa/ byang chub sems dad pa'i rnam par dgod pa la shin tu nges pa rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu rab tu gzhol ba de dag gis de bzhin gshegs pa bstan
36a5(phal chen): ba la ji ltar brtson par byas pa'i rnam pa gang gis/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mnyes par 'gyur ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par dgod pa las 'das par 'gyur
36a6(phal chen): ba dang / spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor chen po yongs su dag par 'gyur ba dang / smon lam chen po yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i gter chen po rab tu thob par 'gyur ba dang / 
36a7(phal chen): sems can rnams la snod ci bzhin du sbyin pa byed par 'gyur ba dang / pha rol tu phyin pa'i phyogs yongs su mi gtong bar 'gyur ba dang / ji ltar dam bcas pa'i sems can rnams sgrol bar 'gyur ba dang / 
36a8(phal chen): sangs rgyas dang / chos dang / dge 'dun gyi gdung mi 'chad par 'gyur ba dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba dmigs pa thams cad du sbyor ba don med par mi 'gyur ba dang / kye rgyal ba'i sras/ byang chub sems
36b1(phal chen): dpa rnams kyis dam dran par byas nas/ rnam pasum 'di dag sangs su chags par 'gyur ba nga skar rtsams par bya ba legs par gagang pa ma tsag/ 'tha da/ thangs cad ni
36b2(phal chen): bar 'dzing ngo // sems can chen por dag gi btsun pa'i rnam pa ji lta dus ma rig pa'i mun dag thams cad bsal te/ bdud kyi dkrugs pa'i 'khor thams cad las shin tu rgyal bar byas
36b3(phal chen): nas/ phas kyi rgol ba thams cad zil gyis mdan te/ sems kyi drim kun nas nyon mongs pa'i phyogs thams cad kun nas bsal nas/ dge ba'i rtsa ba phun sum tshogs pa thams cad shin tu
36b4(phal chen): bsgrubs ste/ mi khoms pa dang / ngan song dang / ngan 'gro'i lam thams cad rnam par bzlog nas/ ye shesakyi dkyil 'khor chen po rnam par byung bar byas te/ byang chu
36b5(phal chen): sems dpa'i sa dang / pha rol tu phyin pa dang gzungs dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / mngon par shes pa dang / rig pa dang / mi 'jigs pa yongs su das / 
36b6(phal chen): pa rnams mngon par bsgrubs nas/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad rnam par dag pa dang / mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po dang / sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi rgyan mngon par sgrub pa yongs su rgyas par
36b7(phal chen): byas te de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi stobs dang / mi 'jigs pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa mnyam pa nyid kyi rjes su song ste/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi yul
36b8(phal chen): rtogs par 'gyur ba dang / de ltar mngon par byang chub nas kyang / bsam pa'i tshul bzhin du/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su grub par gyur pa dag tu ji ltar yongs su smin par bya ba'i sems can
37a1(phal chen): dgal/ dus dang dbang pa'i rgyung ji lta ba bzhid du/ sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa mtha' yas pa 'byin par 'gyur ba de legs par shad cig/ 'khor 'di das thams cad minan
37a2(phal chen): par 'dod ngo // ji ltar yang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis/ byang chub sems dpa'i yon tan 'di dang gzhan dag dang / byang chub sems ngapa'i chos dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dang
37a3(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i lam gyi yul rnams yongs su rdzogs par byas te/ myur du de bzhin gshegs pa'i mnyam pa nyid 'thob pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i
37a4(phal chen): sangs rgyas rnams kyis bskal pa brgya stong grangs med par yang dag par bsgrubs pa'i chos kyi mdzod 'di yang / yang dag par srung zhing byang chub sems dpa'i spyod ba la gnas shing
37a5(phal chen): ston pa dang / 'chad pa'i tshe/ bdud dam/ bdud kyi rigs su gtogs pa dang / phas kyi rgol ba thams cad kyis zil gyis mi non pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad
37a6(phal chen): du yang skyo ba med par dam pa'i chos yongs su 'dzin par byed pa dang / de yang dag par ston pa'i tshe/ lha'i dbang po rnams kyis rim gror bya ba dang / gzhung de bzhin du klu'i dbang po dang / gnod sbyin
37a7(phal chen): gyi dbang po dang / dri za'i dbang po dang / lha ma yin gyi dbang po dang / nam mkha' lding gi dbang po dang / mi 'am ci'i dbang po dang / lto 'phye chen po'i dbang po dang / mi'i dbang po dang / tshangs pa'i
37a8(phal chen): dbang pos rim gror bya ba rab tu 'thob pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa chos kyi dbang pos rim gror bya ba rab tu thob pa dang / de ltar rim gror byas nas kyang 'jig rten thams cad kyis phyag bya ba/ 'jig rten
37b1(phal chen): thams cad kyis mngon par mchod pa 'jig rten thams cad kyi dbang bskur ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis shin tu dgongs pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs kyis shin tu bsrung ba/ rang gi
37b2(phal chen): dge ba'i rtsa ba dang / sngon lams rab tu thob pa/ chos dkar po chen po yang dag par spel ba'i rnams/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi chos kyi mdzod rnam
37b3(phal chen): par 'byed par 'gyur ba dang / dam pa'i chos yongs su 'dzin pa rgyan chen po rab tu 'byed pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i rim gyis spyod pa yongs su bsgrub pa shin tu ston par 'gyur ba de lta bu'i gnas
37b4(phal chen): ngag yang dag par bstan pa mdzod cig/ de nas byang chub sem sa dpa' brtson 'grus blo gros kyis/ don 'di nyid brnam te brjod pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi blo gros la
37b5(phal chen): tshigs su bcad de smras pa/ spyod la 'jug pa mtha' yas yangs/ pa dag/ rang byung ye shes sgrub pa dge ba'i rnams rdzogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' yon tan can// grags
37b6(phal chen): ba chen po rnams la legs par shong // byang chub sems dpa' gang rnams sems thob cing // bsod nams ldan pa ye shes thob pa'i rnams// skyon med zhugs pa 'jig rten rnams bzlog cing / 
37b7(phal chen): yang dag sangs rgyas chos mnyam nyid thob rnams// de dag gis ni bde gshegs bstan pa la// brtson 'gras brtan pas ji ltar brtson par bya// gang gis phyogs bcu'i rgyal ba mnyes
37b8(phal chen): bya zhing rta yang dag sangs rgyas sa'ang gnan bya dang // spyod pa dag dang smon lam yongs dgang dang // ye shes gter chen rab tu 'thob 'gyur zhing // thob nas de dag 'gro kun mi gnas
38a1(phal chen): pas/ yongs su blangs pa rtag tu gtong byed dang // gang yang pha rol phyin pa mchog gi lam// de dag mi gtong rab tu spyod pa dang // sems can ji ltar/ 
38a2(phal chen): sgrol byed dam bcas shing // yang dag sangs rgyas bsam pa mnyam 'dzin dang // mig gi dmigs pa brtan pa thams cad kyi// 'byung ba yon tan can la stobs 'gyur zhing // skyes bu
38a3(phal chen): khyu mchog de dag brtson 'gyur ba'i// rnam dag lam de khyu mchog khyod kyis ston// ji ltar de dag mun pa kun bsal cing // 'khrug pa'i 'khor rnams thams cad pham byas nas// dri ma
38a4(phal chen): bral ba'i dge ldan mkhas pa rnams// skyes bu khyu mchog ye shes ldan 'gyur dang // mi khom ngan song lam rnams yongs spangs shing // ye shes chen po'i dkyil
38a5(phal chen): 'khor mchog sbyong dang // yon tan bzang po thams cadaldan gyur cing // rgyal ba'i ye shes stobs kyanga'athob 'gyur dang // skyes bu khyu mchog ye shes zhugs nas
38a6(phal chen): kyang // sems can bsam pa ji bzhin ston byed cing // mtha' yas yangs pa'i zhing rnams bsam yas su// ston pa chen po'i las kyang byed pa dang // ci nas de dag spyod pa mchog thob
38a7(phal chen): nas/ mi'i khyu mchog mdzod rnams ston byed de// zil gyis ma non gzhan gyis mi 'jam par// rgyal ba'i chos nyid rtag tu 'dzin byed ston// seng ge bzhin du ji ltar 'jig pa med// 
38a8(phal chen): ji ltar zla bzhin dag pa'i mdog tu spyod// chu la pad+mo bzhin du chags med pa// de dag rgyal ba'i yon tan ji ltar sbyong // de skad ces smras pa dang // byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi blo gros
38b1(phal chen): kyis nga byang chub sems dpa' brtson 'grus blo gros la 'di skad ces smras so// kye rgyal ba'i sras// khyon ni skye bo mang po la phan pa dang / skye bo mang po la bde ba dang / 'jig rten la snying brtse ba dang / 
38b2(phal chen): lha dang mi rnams kyi don dang / phan pa dang / bde ba'i phyir zhugs pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras/ khyod de ltar byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa shin tu rtogs shing rnam par dag par brtsams te 'dri zhing / de ltar
38b3(phal chen): rgyal ba'i sras khyod de bzhin gshegs pa dri ba chos mang po la rab tu gnas pa/ brtson 'grus chen pos shin tu bsag pa brtson 'grus ldog pa med pas shin tu byung ba 'dri bar byed pa ni/ kye rgyal ba'i
38b4(phal chen): sras leg so legs so// kye rgyal ba'i sras/ de'i phyir/ da shin tu legs par nyon la yid la zung shig dang / sangs rgyas kyi mthu dang / sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis
38b5(phal chen): phyogs tsam bstan par bya'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di la/ byang chub semams dpa' thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa thob pa rnams kyis/ thog mar sems bskyed
38b6(phal chen): pa de mi nyams par yongs su bsrungs pa dang / rim gror bya ba'i phyir bag yod par bya'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras de la rnam pa bcus ni/ byang chub sems dpa' bag yod pa la gnas pa zhes byas
38b7(phal chen): te/ bcu gang zhe na/ tshul khrims kyi phung po shin tu bsrungs pa dang / byang chub kyi sems ma nyams shing shin tu sbyangs pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i bsam pa g.yo dang sgyu med pa dang / dge ba'i
38b8(phal chen): rtsa ba sbyor ba phyir mi ldog pa dang / rang gi sems bskyed pa shin tu rtogs pa dang / phyogs khyim pa dang / so so'i skye bo dang ma 'dres pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba'i las 'jig rten gyi 'du shes dang 'dod/ 
39a1(phal chen): pa thams cad dang bral ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i lam nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa spangs pa rab tu thob pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba brtsam pa/ nan tan rgyun/ 
39a2(phal chen): chad pa med pa dang / bdag gi rgyud kyi stobs kyi shugs shin tu brtags pa dag ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras rnam pa bcu po 'di dag dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni bag yod pa la gnas pa zhes bya'o// kye rgyal
39a3(phal chen): ba'i sras de la byang chub sems dpag yod pa la gnas pa rnam pa bcus ni// yongasu dag par 'gyur te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di la byang chub sems dpa' ji ltar smras pa de ltar byed pa yin/ 
39a4(phal chen): shes bzhin gyi dran pa can yin/ kheng pa med cing g.yeng ba med de/ bsam gtan zab mo la rab tu gnas pa yin/ sangs rgyas kyi chos zab mo btsal ba la nan tan du byed cing rgyun mi gcod pa
39a5(phal chen): yin/ lhag mthong mngon par bsgrub pa la mkhas shing ji lta 'os pa 'i chos la tshul bzhin du rtog par zhugs pa yin/ bsam gta na gyi rjesu song ba'i sems kyis/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par
39a6(phal chen): 'phrul pa zab mo'i rje su song ba yin/ sa dang mnyam zhing mthon dman dang bral ba yin/ sbyor ba bzang ngan dang bar ma la sems mnyams pa med pa yin/ sems can kun gyi nang na chung ngu na thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du
39a7(phal chen): sems gcig bskyed pa la yang / ston pa'i bsam pa thob pa yin/ mkhan po dang / slob dpon dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen dang / byang chub sems dpa' dang / chos smra ba rnams la rim 'gro dang / bkur ste dang dang / 
39a8(phal chen): tshul can du gnas pa yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras rnam pa bcu po de dag gis/ byang chub sems dpa' ngag yod pa la gnas pa yongasu dag par 'gyu ro// kye rgyal ba'i sras de la byang chub sems dpa' ngag yod pa/ 
39b1(phal chen): brtson 'grus brtsams pa/ dran pa nye bar gnag pa/ mos pa che ba/ rnal 'byor rgyun ma chang ba/ chos thams cad la mi gnas pa/ chos thams cad la brtson pa/ nyon mongs pa med pa'i tshul la zhugs pa/ 
39b2(phal chen): sems yangs pa/ sangs rgyas kyi chos mtha' dang dbus med pa'i rje su song ba rnams kyis ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams mnyes par 'gyur te/ kye rgyal
39b3(phal chen): ba'i sras byang chub sems dpas/ chos bcus de bzhin gshegs pa rnams mnyes par bya'o// bcu gang zhe na/ byang chub sems dpa'i brtson 'grus thams cad la phyir mi ldog pa dang / lus dang srog la mi lta ba
39b4(phal chen): dang / 'tsho ba'i yo byad dang / 'tsho ba'i rkyen la don du gnyer ba med pa dang / chos thams cad rnam par sgom pas/ na mkha' dang mnyam pa dang / chos kyi dbyings la yang dag par gzhol
39b5(phal chen): ba'i lhag mthong la mkhas pa dang / mi gnas pa'i chos rnam par bsgom pa'i phyag rgya dang / rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad par bsgrubs pa'i smon lam chen po dang / yongasu sbyangs pa'i bzod
39b6(phal chen): pa shes pa'i snang ba dang / rang gi dge ba'i chos bsags pa dang / ma bsags pa shin tu brtags pa dang / mngon par 'du bya ba med pa'i sgo shin tu byang ba ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag gis de bzhin
39b7(phal chen): gshegs pa mnyes par bya'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras de la byang chub sems dpa' chos bcu la gnas pa rnams kyis ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnams mnyes par 'gyur ba yin te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 
39b8(phal chen): 'di lta ste/ bag yod pa la gnas pa dang / mi skye ba'i bzod pa la gnas pa dang / snying rje chen po la gnas pa dang / pha rol tu phyin pa yongasasu rdzogs par bya ba gnas pa dang / spyod pa yong su rdzogs
40a1(phal chen): par bya ba la gnas pa dang / smon lam mngon par bsgrub pa la gnas pa dang / thabs mkhas pa la gnas pa dang / brtan pa'i stobs kyi shugs la gnas pa dang / chos thams
40a2(phal chen): cad namakha'i rang bzhin lta bu la rab tu gnas pa dang / len pa med pa la gnas pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras chos de dag la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa mnyes par 'gyur
40a3(phal chen): ro// kye rgyal ba'i sras de la chos bcu dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni/ sa rnam par dgod pa las 'da' ba yin te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs
40a4(phal chen): shin tu bsags pa dang / pha rol tu phyin pa rnam par phye ba tshad med pa'i lam gzhan gyi dring mi 'jog pa'i ye shes snang ba/ dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen dang 'grogs pa rgyun ma chad pa dang / 
40a5(phal chen): brtson 'grus zhig pa med pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyi sa rlabs kyis legs par brlabs pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba sbyor bas mi skyo ba dang / theg pa'i rgyan shin tu bshams pa
40a6(phal chen): dang / ye shes kyi bsam pa rab tu rno ba dang / sa dang sa ma yin pa'i chos kyi sgo la mi gnas pa dang / 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das thams cad dang dge ba'i
40a7(phal chen): rtsa ba rgyud kyi tshul gcig tu gyur pa dag ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras/ chos bcu po de dag gis byang chub sems dpa' rnams sa nas sar rnam par dgod pa las 'da' ba yin no// kye rgyal ba'i sras/ byang chub
40a8(phal chen): sems dpa' de dag ni/ thog ma nas rnam par dgod pa thams cad la mkhas pa rnam par dpyod pa yin te/ chos kyi sgo gang gis gang khong du chud par 'gyur ba dang / ye shes kyi sgo gang gis thob par 'gyur
40b1(phal chen): ba dang / sgrub pa gang yin pa dang / rdzu 'dun pa gang yin pa dang / spyong yul gang yin pa dang / rnam par 'phrul ba gang yin pa dang / yang dag par mthong ba gang yin pa dang / chos kyi sgo rnam par dbye ba'i khyang
40b2(phal chen): par gang yin pa dang / ji ltar thob par bya ba thams cad kyang rnam par dpyod do// de dag la shin tu rnam par dpyad pas/ chos thams cad la mi gnas shing / sems kyi rang bzhin gyis chos thams cad/ 
40b3(phal chen): khong du chud pas/ byang chub sems dpa'i sa yang dag par 'da'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni/ 'di ltar bdag cag gis ci nas kyang myur du 'da' bar bya'o// snyam du mi sems te/ 
40b4(phal chen): de ci'i phyir nen/ 'di ltar de dag 'di snyams du sems te/ 8nga gcags rnas pa la rnam par gnas pas/ ji lta ji ltar yang dag par gnas pa de lta de ltar bsod nams kyi tshogs ches che bskye
40b5(phal chen): bar 'gyur te/ ji lta ji ltar bsod nams kyi tshogs chen po skye sa par gyur pa/ de lta de ltar de bzhin gshegs pa'i sa'i rjes su song zhing sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa tshad med pas nye bar
40b6(phal chen): gnas par 'gyur ro snyam te/ de dag sbyor ba rgyun ma chad cing / skyo ba med pa'i yid dang ldan pa dang / tshogs kyi rgyan chen pos byang chub sems dpa'i sa rnam par dgod pa las yang dag par 'da'o// 
40b7(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras de la byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rnam pa bcus spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor yongasu sbyong bar byas te/ bcu gang zhe na/ yo byad yongasu gzung ba med pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad rim par byed
40b8(phal chen): ba dang / tshul khrims yang dag par blangs pa kha na ma tho ba med pa dang / bzod pa dang nges pa mi zad pa'i sa'i rjesu song ba dang / brtson 'grus rtsom pa/ phyir mi ldog pa'i sbyor ba dang ldan pa dang / dran
41a1(phal chen): pa'i stobs kyi shugs rmongs pa med pa dang / gcig las rnam pa tha dad pa'i chos kyi rjes su song zhing khong du chud ba dang / gnas med pa'i spyod pa bsgrub dka' ba thams cad
41a2(phal chen): la sems ri'i rgyal po lta bu dang / sems can thams cad dang ma 'dres pa'i mu stegs su gyur pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad du sangs rgyas thams cad dang rgyud kyi tshul gcig tu gyur pa ste/ 
41a3(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras rnam pa bcu po de dag gis/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor yongs su sbyang bar bya'o// de dag gi byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa de ltar yongs su sbyangs
41a4(phal chen): ba de rnam pa bcus shin tu dag par 'gyur te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sems ca na gyi gtso bo 'jig rten gyi khams gzhan na bzhugs pas yang dag par dgongs pa dang / 'das
41a5(phal chen): pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i grogs kyisadage ba'i/ rtsa ba bskyed pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs yang dag par gzung ba la mkhas pa dang / dge ba'i
41a6(phal chen): bshes gnyen la yang dag par brten pa dang / mos pa dang / brtson 'grus dang / bag yod pa la rab tu gnas pa dang / chos tha dad pa thams cad la tha mi dang par rtogs pa dang / 
41a7(phal chen): snying rje'i byin gyis brlabs shin tu che ba dang / chos thams cad yang dag par ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par lta ba'i shes rab kyis pha rol tu phyin pa mngon par bsgrub pa dang thabs la mkhas
41a8(phal chen): ba rnam par dpyod pa'i sbyong ba dang / sbyor ba thams cad la de bzhin gshegs pa'i rlabs kyi rjes su 'brang bdag ste/ kyi rgal pa'i sras/ rnam pa bcu po dag gis/ byang chub
41b1(phal chen): sems dpa' rnams kyis spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor yongs su sbyangs par bya'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras de la byang chub sems dpa'i smod lam rnam par dag pa bcu ste/ bcu ga nan/ 'di lta ste
41b2(phal chen): skyo ba med pa sems can gyi khams yongs su smin par bya ba'i smon lam dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba sna tshogs bsags pas/ 'jig rten gyi khams yongs su dag par bya ba'i smon lam dang / 
41b3(phal chen): lus dang srog gis bsngo zhing dam pa'i chos yongs su 'dzin pa'i smon lam dang / ye shes kyi sgo rnam par dpyad pa khong du chung bas/ sangs rgyas kyi gang la 'jug pa'i smon lam dang / byang chub
41b4(phal chen): sems dpa' thams cad dang gnyis su med pas tshul gcig gi rgyud du 'gro ba'i smon lam dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sgo la 'jug pas chos thams cad khong
41b5(phal chen): du chung pa'i smon lam dang / mos pa rnam par spangs pas bstan don yod pa'i smon lam dang / phyi ma'i/ mthar byin gyis brlabs pas bskal par gnas pa'i smon
41b6(phal chen): lam dang / byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i theg pa'i rgyan rnam pa thams cad kyi sgo nas rnam par sbyangs pa'i smon lam dag ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems
41b7(phal chen): dpa' rnams ni de ltar smon lam rnam par sbyong ngo // de dag rnam pa bcus smon lam yongs su rdzogs par byed/ bcu gang zhe na/ yongs su skyo ba med pa dang / rgya chen po mngon

42a4(phal chen): sangs rgyas mthong ba'i gter zad mi shes pa'ang rab tu 'thob bo// gzungs 'khrul pa med pa'i gter zad mi shes pa'ang rab tu 'thob bo// smon lam zad mi

47b4(phal chen): su smin pa'i phyir/ sems can rnams la don du 'gyur/ da ba yin no// kye rgyal ba'i sras/ 'di lta ste dper na/ rtsi'i ming mthong na bde ba zhes bya ba de
47b5(phal chen): mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams kyi lus la zhen pa 'amaltor zos pa'i dug rab tu zhi bar 'gyur ro// kye rgyal ba'i sras/ de bzhin du chos de lta bu dang ldan pa'i
47b6(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' yang mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams kyi nyon mongs pa'i dug thams cad byang bar 'gyur te/ chos dkar po'i stobs kyi shugs kyang skye bar 'gyur ro// kye rgyal ba'i sras
47b7(phal chen): de ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos nyid de lta bu dang ldan zhing chos de dag la gnas te/ shes rab kyi 'od chen pos ma rig pa'i mun pa gsal nas/ bdud kyi dkrugs ma'i
47b8(phal chen): 'khor thams cad byams pa dang snying rje chen po'i stobs kyis pham par byas te/ ye shes dang bsod nams kyi stobs kyi shugs kyis phas kyi rgol ba thams cad zil gyis mnan nas/ rdo rje lta
48a1(phal chen): bu'i ting nge 'dzin la 'jug pas/ sems kyi dri ma thams cad dang / nyon mongs pa'i phyogs thams cad bsal nas/ skyo ba med pa'i skabs dang shugs
48a2(phal chen): kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba phun sum tshogs pa thams cad rab tu sgrub ste/ sngon chad sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su dag par spyad pa'i stobs dang shugs kyi mi khom pa dang ngan song dang ngan 'gro'i lam
48a3(phal chen): thams cad rnam par bzlog nas/ mngon par zhen pa med pa'i stobs dang shugs kyis/ ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor yongs su sbyangs te rim gyi thabs dang shes rab kyi stobs dang shugs
48a4(phal chen): kyis byang chub sems dpa'i sa dang pha rol tu phyin pa dang / ting 'dzin dang mngon par shes pa dang / rig pa dang mi 'jigs pa yongs su dag pa mngon par bsgrubs
48a5(phal chen): nas chos dkar po thams cad kyi stobs dang shugs kyis sangs rgyas thams cad kyi mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po dang / sku dang gsung dang
48a6(phal chen): thugs kyi rgyan yongs su dag pa mngon par bsgrub pa rab tu rgyas par bya ste/ ye shes kyis shes par bya ba'i dbang dang byin gyis brlabs kyis de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs
48a7(phal chen): dang sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa thams cad mnyam pa nyid du khong du chud par byas nas/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyang myur du 'thob cing / thams cad
48a8(phal chen): mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi yul yang smon lam gyi khyad par ji lta ba bzhin du 'thob par 'gyur ro// sngon gyi byin gyi brlabs dang / ye shes kyi byin gyi brlabs kyis mngon par sangs rgyas
48b1(phal chen): nasasems can rnams kyi bsas pa jis pa bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi ningabastan te/ 'dul ba ji lta ba bzhin du sems can rnams la chos kyi 'khor la chen po bskur cing mapar
48b2(phal chen): yas pa'i sems can rnam par 'dul la// kye rgyal ba'i sras/ de ltar byang chub sems dpa'i chos de lta bu dang ldan pa dag ni tshul de lta bus sangs rgyas thams cad dang
48b3(phal chen): nyam pa nyid kyi bar dubab par gyur byang chub sems dpa' snang ba thabasas kyang 'jig rten gyi khams dpa' las bdag tu/ dam pani tsham 'angs
48b4(phal chen): 'dzin cing chos smra ba chen po 'ang byed do// de ltar chos smra ba byed pa'i tshe/ de bzhin gshe/ gas pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas
48b5(phal chen): kyis byin gyis brlabs pa de dag chos kyi mdzod chen gzung zhing bsrung ba'i phyir/ tha dad pa yang dag par shes pas/ chos kyi tshul rab tu dbye ba'i rjes su
48b6(phal chen): song ba'i byang chub sems dpa'i tshig gis 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor mtha' yas par/ bdag gi lus kyi rgyun byin gyis rlabs te bstan pa mngon par bsgrub pa rnam pa'i mchog thams cad
48b7(phal chen): dang ldan pa dang / tha dad pa yang dag par shes pa'i mkhas pa mtha' yas pa dang / ye shes mi zad pa'i sgor 'jug pa dang / dbyangs kyi dkyil 'khor shin tu rnam par
48b8(phal chen): bye ba'i byin gyis rlabs dang / dbyangs gcig bsgrags pas 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad mgu bar byed pa'i dbyangs kyi yan lag rnam par dag pa bsam pa dang / bgal
49a1(phal chen): nyal ba dang / shes pa'i sa ji lta ba bzhin du rjesu 'brang ba dang / lus kyi byin gyis rlabs kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi nang du phyin kyang tshil
49a2(phal chen): gyis mi non pa dang / lus kyi rgyan sgo thams cad du rnam par bstan pa dang / 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi sems dang / bsam pa khong du drung bas/ rab tu rtogs pa dang /

49a4(phal chen): pa med pa'i dbang zhum pa med pa dang / chos kyi dbang zil gyis mi non pa dang / ye shes kyi dbang gzhan gyis mi thub pa dang / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i dbang chos
49a5(phal chen): kyi mtshan nyid 'khrugs pa med pa dang / tha dad pa yang dag par shes pa'i dbang mtshams sbyor ba rgyun chad pa med pa/ ra bsam pa shin tu rtogs pa dang / gzungs kyi dbang chos
49a6(phal chen): thams cad rnam par gdon mi za ba la 'jug pa dang smon lam gyi dbang dpe sna tshogs kyis snyan pa'i tshul nye bar bsgrub pa shin tu bstan pa dang / snying rje chen po'i dbang phyir mi ldog cing rgyun ma
49a7(phal chen): chad pa dang / byams pa chen po'i dbang sngon shin tu skyes pas/ bsam pa thams cad sim par byed pa'i 'od zer gyi dra ba chen po gtong bas chos kyi gtam chen po byed do// de dag ni de bzhin
49a8(phal chen): gshegs pa seng ge'i gdan la bzhugs shing chos kyi gtam gsung ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' ye shes dang smon lam gyi khyad par dang ldan pa ma gtogs par sems can gyi ris na/ byang chub
49b1(phal chen): sems dpa' de la phyir brgal ba 'ang/ spyi gtsug blta ba 'am/ zil gyis gnan pa 'am/ dri ba'i tshogs yongs su dri bas thub par bya bar nus pa'i sems can gang yang med de/ de ni gnas
49b2(phal chen): med do// kye rgyal ba'i sras gal te byang chub sems dpa' dbang de lta bu thob pa la/ 'jig rten gyi khams brjod du med pa tsam du langs pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor cig yod la/ 
49b3(phal chen): 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor de yang sems can stong gsum gyi bdag po'i gzi brjid thob pa sha stag gis gang ba zhig yin na yang / de dag thams cad byang chub sems dpa' 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor du
49b4(phal chen): 'ongs ma thag tu lus bstan pa'i dbang gis zil gyis mnan te/ byams pa chen po'i dbang gis lus kyi gzhi tshim par byas nas/ ye shes chen po'i dbang gi sems dang bsam/ 
49b5(phal chen): pa rnam par shes par bya ste/ mi 'jig pa'i bsam pa/ chen pos chos ston pa byed cing / spobs pa chen po ra// dbang gi sems can tshim par byed do// kye rgyal ba'i
49b6(phal chen): sras de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar byang chub sem sa dpa' de ni ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor tshad med pa dang ldan chos rnam par 'byed pa shin tu rnam par phye ba la mkhas pa
49b7(phal chen): dang ldan dran pa'i stobs dang shugs mnyams shing rgya che ba dang ldan chos thams cad kyi tshul rnam par gdon mi za bar bzung zhing blangs pas rtogs par mkhas pa dang ldan/ byang chub
49b8(phal chen): sems dpa'i thabs mkhas pa mtha' dbus med pa dang ldan/ chos kyi mtshan nyid bsgribs pa med pa'i chos ston pa la mkhas pa dang ldan/ mos pa la mkhas pa sangs rgyas thams cad
50a1(phal chen): kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis blangs pa dang ldan/ dus gsum gyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i dkyil 'khor du yang dag par gzhol ba'i ye shes kyi byin gyis rlabs la mangs/ 
50a2(phal chen): pa dang ldan/ sems can thams cad kyi gtso bo 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba rnams dang / rgyud kyi tshul gcig tu gyur pa'i bsam pa bzang po rnam par dag pa la
50a3(phal chen): mkhas pa dang ldan pas/ chos smra ba chen po byed cing / de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi chos kyi mdzod kyang rnam par 'byed ngo // 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / de ltar byung
50a4(phal chen): ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi ye shes kyi byin gyis rlabs pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i yid kyi smon lam dang / ye na/ sa 'byams klas pas dam pa'i chos kyang yongs su 'dzin to// 
50a5(phal chen): de nas byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi blo gros kyis/ yang byang chub sems dpa' rim gyis yang dag par 'byung / nga'i chos sgo'i le'u yang dag par bstan pa'i phyir sangs rgyas

50b1(phal chen): nimanyes par byed/ brtson 'grus bstan pas bde gshegs mas par byas nas kyang // dus gsum bsad nams tshogs dang yanas ldan pa'i rnams// sa rnams pan rlung phyung
50b2(phal chen): mtshag nyams pa med par byed/ chub pa'i skyon lam rdzogs byed kun pa'ang de bzhin byed/ yi shes gcig la zhugs pa dag zab bya'o/ zab nas 'gro ba kun la myen gyis
50b3(phal chen): tug tang / bsam pa dag dang khams dang sbyar ba zhes byas nas// dbang po je bzhin mkhas pa de ltar chos kyang ston/ pha rom byin la btsun pa mthunan ldan

50b6(phal chen): spyod pa gang yang rung ste spyong pa'i rnams// thams cad don yong rgyal ba rnams kyi sar 'gro'o// de dag ci spyod thams cad 'gro ba rnams la yang // rnam smin don yod nyon mongs drim

50b8(phal chen): sras/ bde gshegs rnams kyi chos rab mdzod kyang rab tu ston// de dag chos spa'i bya ba kun kyang shin tu byed/ bdud rtsi mchog zhim sprin gyi char yang mngon par 'bebs/ 
51a1(phal chen): dngag slong khyams pas 'gro ba kun shang zhing / bta ba de rnams 'khar gyi ma pashes byas nas/ gang gi bsam pabu gras sengs chung ci 'jug

54a5(phal chen): cad kyang 'jig rten gyi khams ming 'di zhes bya ba dag nas 'ongs pa ste/ 'di ltar gnyen dang ldan pa dang me tog dang ldan pa dang / nor dang ldan pa dang

54a7(phal chen): go byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad kyang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan 'di zhes bya ba dag gi zham 'bring na/ tshangs par spyod pa dag ste/ 'di ltar nyams pa med pa'i
54a8(phal chen): spun dang gzhan ma yin pa'i spyan dang / mi g.yo ba'i spyan dang / mi skyod pa'i spyan dang / chu'i spyan dang / bcing pa med pa'i spyan dang / kun tu spod pa'i spyan dang / 
54b1(phal chen): 'od kyi spyan dang ngas pa'i spyan rang mthon ting gi spyan dag go// de nas byang chub sems dpa'adi dag bcom ldan 'das la phyags 'tshal nas sangs rgyas
54b2(phal chen): kyi mthus phyog zu brgyas par byas te/ gang nas 'ongs pa'i phyogs su brtan nas seng ge'i khri rin po che'i snying po can dag bshams te/ skyil mo krung bcas nas 'khod ngo // 
54b3(phal chen): ji ltar gling ba ni pa 'di'i rab mtshe ma'i gnas su byang chub sems dpa' 'ongs par gyur pa de bzhin du/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi gling ba ni ba kun tu yang rab mtshe ma'i
54b4(phal chen): gnas kyi khang pa nor bu sna tshogs su'ang lhags par gyur te/ byang chub sems dpa'i ming yang de skadaces bya ba sha stag/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan kyang
54b5(phal chen): skad ces bya ba'i na 'bring na 'tshangs par spyod pa gsug go// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyi rnabs kyi bol gnyis nas/ 'ong bar bye ba brgya stong bkye ste/ phyogs bcu thams
54b6(phal chen): cad snang bar byas nas 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad bstan te/ byang chub sems dpa' de dag gis 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi gling bzhi pa kun gyi rab mche/ 
54b7(phal chen): ma'i gnas thams cad na yangade bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa yod pa mthong ngo // de nas byang chub sems dpa' yon tan dang ldan pas/ sangs rgyas
54b8(phal chen): kyi mthus phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so// sangs rgyas 'od zer 'ong snang bas// phyogs rnams thams cad rnam par snang / 
55a1(phal chen): des nis sums ma byas pas// mig la ba gang mang yang / mam ga 'anas na/ da gangs pa sa
55a2(phal chen): de bzhin kunan 'ang gsal ba sdang // de ni 'jig rten ngo mngar to// sems can mchob bcu'i rnams// gshegs par gyur pas 'angon par brjod// dadaga'al 'jug
55a3(phal chen): de bzhi kun na rab tu snang // phyogs rnams bcub thams cadan// chos kyi sa parab tus// dekun ming yang nga na te// bangs cas rnams kyi ku rdzob bzhid// 'das ma
55a4(phal chen): kyi ming dag kyang // de zhes bya ba kun nas 'ongs/ gang zag das pa de dag ni// tshangs pa'i spyod pa'ang den spyod// bdag cag rnams la gang btags pa// kun gyi ring yang dang / 
55a5(phal chen): 'thun// sangs rgyas zhing rnams 'dun ldan pa// de dan sangs rgyas rnam 'phrul ba'o// mi'i 'jig rte kun na'ang // 'din rgyal ba bzhugs par shes/ 
55a6(phal chen): gzhan gyis de'i rgyal po yi// gnas na de bzhin bcugs pa mthong ngo // 'jig rter khams rnams thams cad na// gang dag dam pa de bzhugs kyang // rgyal ba mtsham ba gnas
55a7(phal chen): na/ bzhugs par bdag cag kun kyang sems// 'jig rten khams rnams thams cad na// sangs rgyas gzi brjid bsam mi khyab// de dag smon lam bskul ba'i phyir/ 
55a8(phal chen): 'jig rten khams su rab tu bskye// sems can gtso bo'i rnam 'phrul ba// 'di dag de rnams kun gyis mthong // sangs rgyas yon tan mtha' yas te// 'jig rten zang zing thung
55b1(phal chen): bas spangs/ phyogs rnams thams cad kun tu d+d+ha/ chags pa med pa nam par bzhin// de ni gcig las shin tu 'das// mang po dag tu'ang mi dmigs so// mtha las legs
55b2(phal chen): mnga' sangs rgyas rnams// de dag shes par ji ltar rung // gnas pa med cing len pa med// chos dbyings rtogs par thugs su chung // de nas byang chub sems dpa' blo gros dang ldan pas// sangs rgyas
55b3(phal chen): kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis// phyogs bcur rnam par bltas ste// de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so// 'jig rten mgon po 'phrul chen rnams// rdul med gang zag dam pa dag/ 'dus
55b4(phal chen): shing tshogs pa bsam yas pa'i// bskal pa dag tu shin tu dkon// de dag thams cad kun gzigs pa// sems can gtso bo 'ong mdzad de// srog chags kun la phan
55b5(phal chen): pa'i phyir/ sems can rnams la chos ston to// 'jig rten mun nag 'di dag tu// 'jig rten ma/ rapo byung gyur pa// 'jig rten sgron ma de dag ni// blta ba
55b6(phal chen): shin tu dka' ba yin// sbyin pa tshul khrims bzod pa'i rab// brtson 'grus bsam gtan bsgom pa dang // shes rab sngan chad spyad pas na// 'gro ba thams cad snang bar mdzad// sangs rgyas
55b7(phal chen): 'dra ba gang yang med// de phyir de dag mnyam pa med// chos rnams yod pa ma yin pas// skyes bu'i dam pa mthong ba med// sangs rgyas shes rab chen po rnams// mtshan gyi tshogs ni
55b8(phal chen): bsam mi khyab// sku'i tshogs kyis shin tu 'phags// chos rnams kun gyis yang dag byung // 'jig rten grags chen dag pa'i rnams// dnga'ang chen po de dag snang // de dag mtshan tsam thos pas kyang / 
56a1(phal chen): ngan song thams cad spangs par 'gyur// bskal pa rnams ni brjod med par// byang chub don du 'khor byas kyang // 'di'i tshul ni ma shes na// byang chub dan/ 
56a2(phal chen): du zhugs pa min// sangs rgyas bsam gyis mi khyab pa// bskal pa bye bar bkur ba dang // gang gis tshul 'di bsam pa gnyis// 'di ni de las khyad du 'phags// gang gis brjod yas
56a3(phal chen): nang gi rnams// rin chen gang ste thub gsol kyang // 'di'i tshul mi shes na// sangs rgyas byang chub de la ring // de nas byang chub sems dpa' dpal dang ldan pas// sangs rgyas kyis byin gyi ngas
56a4(phal chen): kyis/ phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te// de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so// nam mnga' drim med pa la // nyi ma'i 'od zer mthar las pa// dpyid kyi rdzob tham la// 
56a5(phal chen): phyogs bcu dag tu rab tu snang // de tshe sdig rgyu ci 'dra ga/ de dag bgrang bar mi nus te// mig can rnams kyang de la rmongs// long ba rnams kyi spyod yul mim/ 
56a6(phal chen): de bzhin sems can gtso bo yi// yon tan mtha' dang dbus med pa// bskal pa bsam gyis mi khyab par// sus kyang shes par mi nus so// de dag gang nas blangs pa med// de bzhin
56a7(phal chen): lus kyang byas pa med// de ni tsi las skyes pa med/ rnam par bsgoms na yod pa min/ 'ongs pa med pa'i chos rnams la/ 'gro ba de bzhin mi dmigs te/ de phyir de dag
56a8(phal chen): rgyu yang med// de bzhin 'jig pa'ang yod pa min/ 'jig pa med pa'i chos rnams kyi// rang bzhin/ gang gis shes pa ni// gang la skye ba med pa yi// / yang dag sangs rgyas mthong/ 
56b1(phal chen): bayin/ skyes pa med pa chos rnams // rang nin mangs pa mi rigs te// dadz+ram ngon dugs pas ni// dgas pa med bshes pa yin// 'di ma nas byed gang mang ba/ 
56b2(phal chen): chos rnams thams cad padan nying meng // chos nyid 'dzin gas rdzun/ mangs sunas pa gang yang meng // su ba bar brjod dang smra// dpyir nang rnams rab tu 'dzad// ma
56b3(phal chen): rang bzhin shes gyur na// 'khrug pa med pa rab tu shes/ gang tshe 'jig rten zhing yin par// tshul bzhin du ni rtog byed na/ de thathams cad dor bstan pa/ byang chub sems dpas
56b4(phal chen): rab tu shes// de nas byang chub sems dpa' dga' ba dang lnga dan pas/ sangs rgyas kyi mthus phyogs bcur rnam par bltas ste/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag
56b5(phal chen): smras so// gnas 'di shin tu rgya che ste/ chos kyi dbye ngas kyis klas pa yin/ rtag tu kun tu song ba ste// yid du 'ong zhing gnas kyang med// de la yang dag
56b6(phal chen): brtag byas shing // rim gro yod par dang byed na// sdug bsngal nam yang mi mthong ste// ngan song rnams kyang mi mthong ngo // tshang med de bzhin grangs med pa'i// 'jig rten khams su su
56b7(phal chen): 'gro bas// gang rnams 'dir snang ba yi// sangs rgyas byin rlabs thos par 'gyur// drang song chen po'i byin gyi rlabs// gang gis thos par gyur nas kyang // 'di 'dra sangs rgyas
56b8(phal chen): chos so zhes// rtog med bla med byang chub bo// gang rnams 'das pa'i sangs rgyas kyis/ chos nyid la ni yid ces pa/ de kun 'jig rten sgron ma ste/ rkang gnyis ldan
57a1(phal chen): pa'i dam par 'gyur// sangs rgyas rnam par 'phrul ba 'di// la la zhig gis thos gyur cing // thos nas dang par byed 'gyur na// de dag mi'i dam par 'gyur/ 
57a2(phal chen): brtan pa gang rnams da ltar yang // sangs rgyas chos la dang byed pa// de dag don gzigs mi 'jigs pa'i// de bzhin gshegs par 'gyur ba yin// bskal pa bsam gyis mi khyab par// 
57a3(phal chen): 'di 'dra thos pa shin tu dkon// smon lam dbang ni mi gtogs par// blo gros 'di 'drar 'gyur ba min// sangs rgyas dam chos 'di las kyang // legs par bshad pa bzung byas shing /

57a5(phal chen): brjod pa yi// shes pa 'di 'dra mnyan par bya/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' 'khril dang ldan pas/ sangs rgyas kyis byin gyi rlangs kyis// phyogs bcur
57a6(phal chen): rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcas de smras pa// gang zhig thos nas 'di 'dra ba'i// dga' ba yangs pa skye ba dang // the tsom rnam par 'chang ba ni// 'jig rten na ni ngo mtshar
57a7(phal chen): che/ 'di ltar thams cad gzigs pa'i rnams// nyid kyi 'gro la bka' stsal na// sangs rgyas mi mkhyen gang yang med// de ltar sangs rgyas bsam mi khyab// mi shes pa yi rgyu las ni/ 
57a8(phal chen): legs 'jug par mi 'gyur te/ mun pa'i mthung nga snang ba gnyig/ lhan cig 'byung bami 'gyur btan// ji mar gzugs dang gzugs med pa/ brgal pa mnyam pa med par
57b1(phal chen): bshad/ de ltar shes dang mi shes pa// 'grogs par shin tu mi 'gyur ro// 'khor dang mya ngan 'das pa dag/ ji ltar med la sa brtags paltar// de bzhin shes dang mi shes pa/ mtshan
57b2(phal chen): nyid bzhin du dmigs pa med// ji ltar 'jig rten 'jig pa dang // 'du bar 'gyur ba ring ba ste// phan tshun 'grogs par mi 'gyur ba// shes dang mi shes de bzhin no// ji ltar byang
57b3(phal chen): chub sems dpa' mi// thog ma'i sems dang tha ma'i sems// lhan cig mi gnas byung ba ltar// shes dang mi shes de bzhin no// ji ltar lus dang rnam shes pa// gzhan dang gzhan
57b4(phal chen): las 'byung 'gyu rab// de bzhin shes dang mi shes gnyis// 'grogs par 'gyur ba nam yang med// ji ltaradug la phan pa'i rtse// 'phral du drug ni dug min byed/

58a1(phal chen): bzhin med// bdags su med las byung ba ltar// chos rnams rang bzhin de bzhin no// ma 'ongs dus ni ji lta bur// 'das pas brjod par bya ba ste// de la

59b2(phal chen): khams rnams ma gtogs gzhan na yang // tshon ces bya ba gang yang med// sems la ri mo med de// ri mo la'ang sems med do// sems de ma gtogs gzhin du'ang // ri mo gang yang mi
59b3(phal chen): dmigs so// sems de rtag pa ma yin pa// bsam gyis mi khyab tshad med cing // phan tshun shes pa med pa yi// gzugs rnams thams cad ston par byed// ji ltar ri mo mkhan gyi rnams//

60a1(phal chen): mthus/ phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad de smras pa/ gzung du med la 'dzin ces bya/ snang ba med pa snang ba ste// mnyan du med par nyan
60a2(phal chen): par byed/ sems med pa'i sems dang ldan// tshad med pa la tshad ma yis// gang zhig 'dzin par mi 'dod pa// de ni tshad med tshad ma yis// nam yang 'dzin par mi 'gyur ro//
